 329→\tlogger := api.requestLogger(params.HTTPRequest)\n   330→\n   331→\tctx, span := tracer.Start(params.HTTPRequest.Context(), \"api.postAlertsHandler\")\n   332→\tdefer span.End()\n   333→\n 360→\t\t\tapi.m.Firing().Inc()\n   361→\t\t} else {\n   362→\t\t\tapi.m.Resolved().Inc()\n   363→\t\t}\n   364→\t}\n   365→\n   366→\t// Make a best effort to insert all alerts that are valid.\n   367→\tvar (\n   368→\t\tvalidAlerts    = make([]*types.Alert, 0, len(alerts))\n   369→\t\tvalidationErrs error\n   370→\t)\n   371→\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n   372→\t\tremoveEmptyLabels(a.Labels)\n   373→\n   374→\t\tif err := a.Validate(); err != nil {\n   375→\t\t\tvalidationErrs = errors.Join(validationErrs, err)\n   376→\t\t\tapi.m.Invalid().Inc()\n   377→\t\t\tcontinue\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t\tvalidAlerts = append(validAlerts, a)\n   380→\t}\n   381→\tif err := api.alerts.Put(ctx, validAlerts...); err != nil {\n   382→\t\tmessage := \"Failed to 391→\t\tlogger.Error(message, \"err\", validationErrs.Error())\n   392→\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, message)\n   393→\t\tspan.RecordError(validationErrs)\n   394→\t\treturn alert_ops.NewPostAlertsBadRequest().WithPayload(validationErrs.Error())\n   395→\t}\n   396→\n   397→\treturn alert_ops.NewPostAlertsOK()\n   398→}\n   399→\n   400→func (api *API) 470→}\n   471→\n   472→func (api *API) alertFilter(matchers []*labels.Matcher, silenced, inhibited, active bool) func(a *types.Alert, now time.Time) bool {\n   473→\treturn func(a *types.Alert, now time.Time) bool {\n   474→\t\tctx, span := tracer.Start(context.Background(), \"alertFilter\")\n   475→\t\tdefer span.End()\n   476→\n   477→\t\tif !a.EndsAt.IsZero() && a.EndsAt.Before(now) {\n   478→\t\t\treturn false\n   479→\t\t}\n   480→\n   481→\t\t// Set alert's current status based on its label set.\n   482→\t\tapi.setAlertStatus(ctx, a.Labels)\n   483→\n   484→\t\t// Get alert's current status after seeing if it is suppressed.\n   485→\t\tstatus := api.getAlertStatus(a.Fingerprint())\n   486→\n   487→\t\tif !active && status.State == types.AlertStateActive {\n   488→\t\t\treturn false\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\n   491→\t\tif !silenced && len(status.SilencedBy) != 0 {\n   492→\t\t\treturn false\n   493→\t\t}\n   494→\n   495→\t\tif !inhibited && len(status.InhibitedBy) != 0 {\n   496→\t\t\treturn false\n   497→\t\t}\n   498→\n   499→\t\treturn alertMatchesFilterLabels(&a.Alert, matchers)\n   500→\t}\n   501→}\n   502→\n   503→func removeEmptyLabels(ls prometheus_model.LabelSet) {\n   504→\tfor k, v := range ls {\n   505→\t\tif string(v) == \"\" {\n   506→\t\t\tdelete(ls, k)\n   507→\t\t}\n   508→\t}\n   509→}\n   510→\n   511→func alertMatchesFilterLabels(a *prometheus_model.Alert, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n   512→\tsms := make(map[string]string)\n   513→\tfor name, value := range a.Labels {\n   514→\t\tsms[string(name)] = string(value)\n   515→\t}\n   516→\treturn matchFilterLabels(matchers, sms)\n   517→}\n   518→\n   519→func matchFilterLabels(matchers []*labels.Matcher, sms map[string]string) bool {\n   520→\tfor _, m := range matchers {\n   521→\t\tv, prs := sms[m.Name]\n   522→\t\tswitch m.Type {\n   523→\t\tcase labels.MatchNotRegexp, labels.MatchNotEqual:\n   524→\t\t\tif m.Value == \"\" && prs {\n   525→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   526→\t\t\t}\n   527→\t\t\tif !m.Matches(v) {\n   528→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   529→\t\t\t}\n   530→\t\tdefault:\n   531→\t\t\tif m.Value == \"\" && !prs {\n   532→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   533→\t\t\t}\n   534→\t\t\tif !m.Matches(v) {\n   535→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   536→\t\t\t}\n   537→\t\t}\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\treturn true\n   541→}\n   542→\n   543→func (api *API) getSilencesHandler(params silence_ops.GetSilencesParams) middleware.Responder {\n   544→\tlogger := api.requestLogger(params.HTTPRequest)\n   545→\n   546→\tctx, span := tracer.Start(params.HTTPRequest.Context(), \"api.getSilencesHandler\")\n   547→\tdefer span.End()\n   548→\n   549→\tmatchers, err := parseFilter(params.Filter)\n   550→\tif err != nil {\n   551→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Failed to parse matchers\", \"err\", err)\n   552→\t\treturn silence_ops.NewGetSilencesBadRequest().WithPayload(err.Error())\n   553→\t}\n   554→\n   555→\tpsils, _, err := api.silences.Query(ctx)\n   556→\tif err != nil {\n   557→\t\tlogger.Error(\"Failed to get silences\", \"err\", err)\n   558→\t\treturn silence_ops.NewGetSilencesInternalServerError().WithPayload(err.Error())\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\tsils := open_api_models.GettableSilences{}\n   562→\tfor _, ps := range psils {\n   563→\t\tif !CheckSilenceMatchesFilterLabels(ps, matchers) {\n   564→\t\t\tcontinue\n   565→\t\t}\n   566→\t\tsilence, err := GettableSilenceFromProto(ps)\n   567→\t\tif err != nil {\n   568→\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"Failed to unmarshal silence from proto\", \"err\", err)\n   569→\t\t\treturn silence_ops.NewGetSilencesInternalServerError().WithPayload(err.Error())\n   570→\t\t}\n   571→\t\tsils = append(sils, &silence)\n   572→\t}\n   573→\n   574→\tSortSilences(sils)\n   575→\n   576→\treturn silence_ops.NewGetSilencesOK().WithPayload(sils)\n   577→}\n   578→\n   579→var silenceStateOrder = map[silence.SilenceState]int{\n   580→\tsilence.SilenceStateActive:  1,\n   581→\tsilence.SilenceStatePending: 2,\n   582→\tsilence.SilenceStateExpired: 3,\n   583→}\n   584→\n   585→// SortSilences sorts first according to the state \"active, pending, expired\"\n   586→// then by end time or start time depending on the state.\n   587→// Active silences should show the next to expire first\n   588→// pending silences are ordered based on which one starts next\n   589→// expired are ordered based on which one expired most recently.\n   590→func SortSilences(sils open_api_models.GettableSilences) {\n   591→\tsort.Slice(sils, func(i, j int) bool {\n   592→\t\tstate1 := silence.SilenceState(*sils[i].Status.State)\n   593→\t\tstate2 := silence.SilenceState(*sils[j].Status.State)\n   594→\t\tif state1 != state2 {\n   595→\t\t\treturn silenceStateOrder[state1] < silenceStateOrder[state2]\n   596→\t\t}\n   597→\t\tswitch state1 {\n   598→\t\tcase silence.SilenceStateActive:\n   599→\t\t\tendsAt1 := time.Time(*sils[i].EndsAt)\n   600→\t\t\tendsAt2 := time.Time(*sils[j].EndsAt)\n   601→\t\t\treturn endsAt1.Before(endsAt2)\n   602→\t\tcase silence.SilenceStatePending:\n   603→\t\t\tstartsAt1 := time.Time(*sils[i].StartsAt)\n   604→\t\t\tstartsAt2 := time.Time(*sils[j].StartsAt)\n   605→\t\t\treturn startsAt1.Before(startsAt2)\n   606→\t\tcase silence.SilenceStateExpired:\n   607→\t\t\tendsAt1 := time.Time(*sils[i].EndsAt)\n   608→\t\t\tendsAt2 := time.Time(*sils[j].EndsAt)\n   609→\t\t\treturn endsAt1.After(endsAt2)\n   610→\t\t}\n   611→\t\treturn false\n   612→\t})\n   613→}\n   614→\n   615→// CheckSilenceMatchesFilterLabels returns true if\n   616→// a given silence matches a list of matchers.\n   617→// A silence matches a filter (list of matchers) if\n   618→// for all matchers in the filter, there exists a matcher in the silence\n   619→// such that their names, types, and values are equivalent.\n   620→func CheckSilenceMatchesFilterLabels(s *silencepb.Silence, matchers []*labels.Matcher) bool {\n   621→\t// Check if any matcher set matches (OR logic)\n   622→\tfor _, validationErrs.Error())\n\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, message)\n\t\tspan.RecordError(validationErrs)\n\t\treturn 134→\troute *Route,\n   135→\tstage notify.Stage,\n   136→\tmarker types.GroupMarker,\n   137→\ttimeout func(time.Duration) time.Duration,\n   138→\tmaintenanceInterval time.Duration,\n   139→\tlimits Limits,\n   140→\tlogger *slog.Logger,\n   141→\tmetrics *DispatcherMetrics,\n   142→) *Dispatcher {\n   143→\tif limits == nil {\n   144→\t\tlimits = nilLimits{}\n   145→\t}\n   146→\n   147→\t// Calculate concurrency for ingestion.\n   148→\tconcurrency := min(max(runtime.GOMAXPROCS(0)/2, 2), 8)\n   149→\n   150→\tdisp := &Dispatcher{\n   151→\t\talerts:              alerts,\n   152→\t\tstage:               stage,\n   153→\t\troute:               route,\n   154→\t\tmarker:              marker,\n   155→\t\ttimeout:             timeout,\n   156→\t\tmaintenanceInterval: maintenanceInterval,\n   157→\t\tconcurrency:         concurrency,\n   158→\t\tlogger:              logger.With(\"component\", \"dispatcher\"),\n   159→\t\tmetrics:             metrics,\n   160→\t\tlimits:              limits,\n   161→\t\tpropagator:          otel.GetTextMapPropagator(),\n   162→\t}\n   163→\tdisp.state.Store(DispatcherStateUnknown)\n   164→\tdisp.loaded = make(chan struct{})\n   165→\tdisp.ctx, disp.cancel = context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n   166→\treturn disp\n   167→}\n   168→\n   169→// Run starts dispatching alerts incoming via the updates channel.\n   170→func (d *Dispatcher) Run(dispatchStartTime time.Time) {\n   171→\tif !d.state.CompareAndSwap(DispatcherStateUnknown, DispatcherStateWaitingToStart) {\n   172→\t\treturn\n   173→\t}\n   174→\td.finished.Add(1)\n   175→\tdefer d.finished.Done()\n   176→\n   177→\td.logger.Debug(\"preparing to start\", \"startTime\", dispatchStartTime)\n   178→\td.startTimer = time.NewTimer(time.Until(dispatchStartTime))\n   179→\td.logger.Debug(\"setting state\", \"state\", \"waiting_to_start\")\n   180→\td.routeGroupsSlice = make([]routeAggrGroups, d.route.Idx+1)\n   181→\td.route.Walk(func(r *Route) {\n   182→\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[r.Idx] = routeAggrGroups{\n   183→\t\t\troute: r,\n   184→\t\t}\n   185→\t})\n   186→\n   187→\td.aggrGroupsNum.Store(0)\n   188→\td.metrics.aggrGroups.Set(0)\n   189→\n   190→\tinitalAlerts, it := d.alerts.SlurpAndSubscribe(\"dispatcher\")\n   191→\tfor _, alert := range initalAlerts {\n   192→\t\td.routeAlert(d.ctx, alert)\n   193→\t}\n   194→\tclose(d.loaded)\n   195→\n   196→\td.run(it)\n   197→}\n   198→\n   199→func (d *Dispatcher) run(it provider.AlertIterator) {\n   200→\tdefer it.Close()\n   201→\n   202→\t// Start maintenance goroutine\n   203→\td.finished.Go(func() {\n   204→\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(d.maintenanceInterval)\n   205→\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n   206→\n   207→\t\tfor {\n   208→\t\t\tselect {\n   209→\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n   210→\t\t\t\td.doMaintenance()\n   211→\t\t\tcase <-d.ctx.Done():\n   212→\t\t\t\treturn\n   213→\t\t\t}\n   214→\t\t}\n   215→\t})\n   216→\n   217→\t// Start timer goroutine\n   218→\td.finished.Go(func() {\n   219→\t\t<-d.startTimer.C\n   220→\n   221→\t\tif d.state.CompareAndSwap(DispatcherStateWaitingToStart, DispatcherStateRunning) {\n   222→\t\t\td.logger.Debug(\"started\", \"state\", \"running\")\n   223→\t\t\td.logger.Debug(\"Starting all existing aggregation groups\")\n   224→\t\t\tfor rg := range d.routeGroupsSlice {\n   225→\t\t\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[rg].groups.Range(func(_, ag any) bool {\n   226→\t\t\t\t\td.runAG(ag.(*aggrGroup))\n   227→\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n   228→\t\t\t\t})\n   229→\t\t\t}\n   230→\t\t}\n   231→\t})\n   232→\n   233→\t// Start multiple alert ingestion goroutines\n   234→\talertCh := it.Next()\n   235→\tfor i := 0; i < d.concurrency; i++ {\n   236→\t\td.finished.Add(1)\n   237→\t\tgo func(workerID int) {\n   238→\t\t\tdefer d.finished.Done()\n   239→\t\t\td.logger.Debug(\"starting alert ingestion worker\", \"workerID\", workerID)\n   240→\n   241→\t\t\tfor {\n   242→\t\t\t\tselect {\n   243→\t\t\t\tcase alert, ok := <-alertCh:\n   244→\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   245→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Iterator exhausted for some reason.\n   246→\t\t\t\t\t\tif err := it.Err(); err != nil {\n   247→\t\t\t\t\t\t\td.logger.Error(\"Error on alert update\", \"err\", err, \"workerID\", workerID)\n   248→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   249→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   250→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   251→\n   252→\t\t\t\t\t// Log errors but keep trying.\n   253→\t\t\t\t\tif err := it.Err(); err != nil {\n   254→\t\t\t\t\t\td.logger.Error(\"Error on alert update\", \"err\", err, \"workerID\", workerID)\n   255→\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   256→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   257→\n   258→\t\t\t\t\tctx := d.ctx\n   259→\t\t\t\t\tif alert.Header != nil {\n   260→\t\t\t\t\t\tctx = d.propagator.Extract(ctx, propagation.MapCarrier(alert.Header))\n   261→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   262→\n   263→\t\t\t\t\td.routeAlert(ctx, alert.Data)\n   264→\n   265→\t\t\t\tcase <-d.ctx.Done():\n   266→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   267→\t\t\t\t}\n   268→\t\t\t}\n   269→\t\t}(i)\n   270→\t}\n   271→\t<-d.ctx.Done()\n   272→}\n   273→\n   274→func (d *Dispatcher) routeAlert(ctx context.Context, alert *types.Alert) {\n   275→\td.logger.Debug(\"Received alert\", \"alert\", alert)\n   276→\n   277→\tctx, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"dispatch.Dispatcher.routeAlert\",\n   278→\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   279→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.alert.name\", alert.Name()),\n   280→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.alert.fingerprint\", alert.Fingerprint().String()),\n   281→\t\t),\n   282→\t\ttrace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindInternal),\n   283→\t)\n   284→\tdefer span.End()\n   285→\n   286→\tnow := time.Now()\n   287→\tfor _, r := range d.route.Match(alert.Labels) {\n   288→\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"dispatching alert to route\",\n   289→\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   290→\t\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.route.receiver.name\", r.RouteOpts.Receiver),\n   291→\t\t\t),\n   292→\t\t)\n   293→\t\td.groupAlert(ctx, alert, r)\n   294→\t}\n   295→\td.metrics.processingDuration.Observe(time.Since(now).Seconds())\n   296→}\n   297→\n   298→func (d *Dispatcher) doMaintenance() {\n   299→\tfor i := range d.routeGroupsSlice {\n   300→\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[i].groups.Range(func(_, el any) bool {\n   301→\t\t\tag := el.(*aggrGroup)\n   302→\t\t\tif ag.destroyed() {\n   303→\t\t\t\tag.stop()\n   304→\t\t\t\td.marker.DeleteByGroupKey(ag.routeID, ag.GroupKey())\n   305→\t\t\t\tdeleted := d.routeGroupsSlice[i].groups.CompareAndDelete(ag.fingerprint(), ag)\n   306→\t\t\t\tif deleted {\n   307→\t\t\t\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[i].groupsLen.Add(-1)\n   308→\t\t\t\t\td.aggrGroupsNum.Add(-1)\n   309→\t\t\t\t\td.metrics.aggrGroups.Set(float64(d.aggrGroupsNum.Load()))\n   310→\t\t\t\t}\n   311→\t\t\t}\n   312→\t\t\treturn true\n   313→\t\t})\n   314→\t}\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→func (d *Dispatcher) WaitForLoading() {\n   318→\t<-d.loaded\n   319→}\n   320→\n   321→func (d *Dispatcher) LoadingDone() <-chan struct{} {\n   322→\treturn d.loaded\n   323→}\n   324→\n   325→// AlertGroup represents how alerts exist within an aggrGroup.\n   326→type AlertGroup struct {\n   327→\tAlerts   types.AlertSlice\n   328→\tLabels   model.LabelSet\n   329→\tReceiver string\n   330→\tGroupKey string\n   331→\tRouteID  string\n   332→}\n   333→\n   334→type AlertGroups []*AlertGroup\n   335→\n   336→func (ag AlertGroups) Swap(i, j int) { ag[i], ag[j] = ag[j], ag[i] }\n   337→func (ag AlertGroups) Less(i, j int) bool {\n   338→\tif ag[i].Labels.Equal(ag[j].Labels) {\n   339→\t\treturn ag[i].Receiver < ag[j].Receiver\n   340→\t}\n   341→\treturn ag[i].Labels.Before(ag[j].Labels)\n   342→}\n   343→func (ag AlertGroups) Len() int { return len(ag) }\n   344→\n   345→// Groups returns a slice of AlertGroups from the dispatcher's internal state.\n   346→func (d *Dispatcher) Groups(ctx context.Context, routeFilter func(*Route) bool, alertFilter func(*types.Alert, time.Time) bool) (AlertGroups, map[model.Fingerprint][]string, error) {\n   347→\tselect {\n   348→\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   349→\t\treturn nil, nil, ctx.Err()\n   350→\tcase <-d.LoadingDone():\n   351→\t}\n   352→\tgroups := AlertGroups{}\n   353→\n   354→\t// Keep a list of receivers for an alert to prevent checking each alert\n   355→\t// again against all routes. The alert has already matched against this\n   356→\t// route on ingestion.\n   357→\treceivers := map[model.Fingerprint][]string{}\n   358→\n   359→\tnow := time.Now()\n   360→\tfor i := range d.routeGroupsSlice {\n   361→\t\tif !routeFilter(d.routeGroupsSlice[i].route) {\n   362→\t\t\tcontinue\n   363→\t\t}\n   364→\t\treceiver := d.routeGroupsSlice[i].route.RouteOpts.Receiver\n   365→\n   366→\t\t// Make a snapshot of the aggregation groups in each route to avoid holding\n   367→\t\t// sync.Map locks while we process alerts or acquiring leaf locks in the alert\n   368→\t\t// store.\n   369→\n   370→\t\t// Estimate capacity based on total groups and number of routes.\n   371→\t\t// We overallocate a bit to avoid copying in most cases.\n   372→\t\tsnapshot := make([]*aggrGroup, 0, d.routeGroupsSlice[i].groupsLen.Load()+32)\n   373→\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[i].groups.Range(func(_, el any) bool {\n   374→\t\t\tsnapshot = append(snapshot, el.(*aggrGroup))\n   375→\t\t\treturn true\n   376→\t\t})\n   377→\n   378→\t\t// Process the snapshot without holding sync.Map locks\n   379→\t\tfor _, ag := range snapshot {\n   380→\t\t\talertGroup := &AlertGroup{\n   381→\t\t\t\tLabels:   ag.labels,\n   382→\t\t\t\tReceiver: receiver,\n   383→\t\t\t\tGroupKey: ag.GroupKey(),\n   384→\t\t\t\tRouteID:  ag.routeID,\n   385→\t\t\t}\n   386→\n   387→\t\t\talerts := ag.alerts.List()\n   388→\t\t\tfilteredAlerts := make([]*types.Alert, 0, len(alerts))\n   389→\t\t\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n   390→\t\t\t\tif !alertFilter(a, now) {\n   391→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   392→\t\t\t\t}\n   393→\n   394→\t\t\t\tfp := a.Fingerprint()\n   395→\t\t\t\tif r, ok := receivers[fp]; ok {\n   396→\t\t\t\t\t// Receivers slice already exists. Add\n   397→\t\t\t\t\t// the current receiver to the slice.\n   398→\t\t\t\t\treceivers[fp] = append(r, receiver)\n   399→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   400→\t\t\t\t\t// First time we've seen this alert fingerprint.\n   401→\t\t\t\t\t// Initialize a new receivers slice.\n   402→\t\t\t\t\treceivers[fp] = []string{receiver}\n   403→\t\t\t\t}\n   404→\n   405→\t\t\t\tfilteredAlerts = append(filteredAlerts, a)\n   406→\t\t\t}\n   407→\t\t\tif len(filteredAlerts) == 0 {\n   408→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   409→\t\t\t}\n   410→\t\t\talertGroup.Alerts = filteredAlerts\n   411→\n   412→\t\t\tgroups = append(groups, alertGroup)\n   413→\t\t}\n   414→\t}\n   415→\tsort.Sort(groups)\n   416→\tfor i := range groups {\n   417→\t\tsort.Sort(groups[i].Alerts)\n   418→\t}\n   419→\tfor i := range receivers {\n   420→\t\tsort.Strings(receivers[i])\n   421→\t}\n   422→\n   423→\treturn groups, receivers, nil\n   424→}\n   425→\n   426→// Stop the dispatcher.\n   427→func (d *Dispatcher) Stop() {\n   428→\tif d == nil {\n   429→\t\treturn\n   430→\t}\n   431→\td.state.Store(DispatcherStateStopped)\n   432→\td.cancel()\n   433→\td.finished.Wait()\n   434→}\n   435→\n   436→// notifyFunc is a function that performs notification for the alert\n   437→// with the given fingerprint. It aborts on context cancelation.\n   438→// Returns false if notifying failed.\n   439→type notifyFunc func(context.Context, ...*types.Alert) bool\n   440→\n   441→// groupAlert determines in which aggregation group the alert falls\n   442→// and inserts it.\n   443→func (d *Dispatcher) groupAlert(ctx context.Context, alert *types.Alert, route *Route) {\n   444→\t_, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"dispatch.Dispatcher.groupAlert\",\n   445→\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   446→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.alert.name\", alert.Name()),\n   447→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.alert.fingerprint\", alert.Fingerprint().String()),\n   448→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.route.receiver.name\", route.RouteOpts.Receiver),\n   449→\t\t),\n   450→\t\ttrace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindInternal),\n   451→\t)\n   452→\tdefer span.End()\n   453→\n   454→\tnow := time.Now()\n   455→\tgroupLabels := getGroupLabels(alert, route)\n   456→\n   457→\tfp := groupLabels.Fingerprint()\n   458→\n   459→\tel, loaded := d.routeGroupsSlice[route.Idx].groups.Load(fp)\n   460→\tif loaded {\n   461→\t\tag := el.(*aggrGroup)\n   462→\t\t// Try to insert into the aggrgroup.\n   463→\t\t// If it's destroyed insert will return false.\n   464→\t\tif ag.insert(ctx, alert) {\n   465→\t\t\treturn\n   466→\t\t}\n   467→\t}\n   468→\n   469→\t// If we couldn't insert, we need to create a new aggregation group.\n   470→\t// Since multiple goroutines might be trying to create the same group concurrently\n   471→\t// we will use the sync map swap to ensure only one of them creates it.\n   472→\n   473→\t// If the group does not exist, create it. But check the limit first.\n   474→\tlimit := d.limits.MaxNumberOfAggregationGroups()\n   475→\tcurrent := int(d.aggrGroupsNum.Load())\n   476→\tif limit > 0 && current >= limit {\n   477→\t\td.metrics.aggrGroupLimitReached.Inc()\n   478→\t\terr := errors.New(\"too many aggregation groups, cannot create new group for alert\")\n   479→\t\tmessage := \"Failed to create aggregation group\"\n   480→\t\td.logger.Error(message, \"err\", err.Error(), \"groups\", current, \"limit\", limit, \"alert\", alert.Name())\n   481→\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, message)\n   482→\t\tspan.RecordError(err,\n   483→\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   484→\t\t\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.aggregation_group.count\", current),\n   485→\t\t\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.aggregation_group.limit\", limit),\n   486→\t\t\t),\n   487→\t\t)\n   488→\t\treturn\n   489→\t}\n   490→\n   491→\tag := newAggrGroup(d.ctx, groupLabels, route, d.timeout, d.marker.(types.AlertMarker), d.logger)\n   492→\t// Insert the 1st alert in the group before starting the group's run()\n   493→\t// function, to make sure that when the run() will be executed the 1st\n   494→\t// alert is already there.\n   495→\tag.insert(ctx, alert)\n   496→\n   497→\tretries := 0\n   498→\tfor {\n   499→\t\tif loaded {\n   500→\t\t\t// Try to store the new group in the map. If another goroutine has already created the same group, use the existing one.\n   501→\t\t\tswapped := d.routeGroupsSlice[route.Idx].groups.CompareAndSwap(fp, el, ag)\n   502→\t\t\tif swapped {\n   503→\t\t\t\t// We swapped the new group in, we can break and start it.\n   504→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   505→\t\t\t}\n   506→\t\t} else {\n   507→\t\t\tel, loaded = d.routeGroupsSlice[route.Idx].groups.LoadOrStore(fp, ag)\n   508→\t\t\tif !loaded {\n   509→\t\t\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[route.Idx].groupsLen.Add(1)\n   510→\t\t\t\td.aggrGroupsNum.Add(1)\n   511→\t\t\t\td.metrics.aggrGroups.Set(float64(d.aggrGroupsNum.Load()))\n   512→\t\t\t\t// We stored the new group, we can break and start it.\n   513→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   514→\t\t\t}\n   515→\t\t\tif el == nil {\n   516→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   517→\t\t\t}\n   518→\t\t\t// we found an existing group, try to insert the alert into it. If it's destroyed, we will retry the whole process with the updated el.\n   519→\t\t\tagExisting := el.(*aggrGroup)\n   520→\t\t\tif agExisting.insert(ctx, alert) {\n   521→\t\t\t\treturn // if we inserted we return to avoid incrementing the aggrgroup count and starting the group.\n   522→\t\t\t}\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\n   525→\t\t// If we failed to swap, it means another goroutine has created/modified the group\n   526→\t\tretries++\n   527→\t\tif retries > 100 {\n   528→\t\t\t// This shouldn't happen - indicates a bug or extreme contention\n   529→\t\t\td.logger.Error(\"excessive retries creating aggregation group\",\n   530→\t\t\t\t\"fingerprint\", fp,\n   531→\t\t\t\t\"route\", route.Key(),\n   532→\t\t\t\t\"alert\", alert.Name(),\n   533→\t\t\t\t\"retries\", retries,\n   534→\t\t\t)\n   535→\t\t\t// Give up and accept potential alert loss rather than infinite loop\n   536→\t\t\treturn\n   537→\t\t}\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\tspan.AddEvent(\"new AggregationGroup created\",\n   541→\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   542→\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.aggregation_group.key\", ag.GroupKey()),\n   543→\t\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.aggregation_group.count\", int(d.aggrGroupsNum.Load())),\n   544→\t\t),\n   545→\t)\n   546→\n   547→\tif alert.StartsAt.Add(ag.opts.GroupWait).Before(now) {\n   548→\t\tmessage := \"Alert is old enough for immediate flush, resetting timer to zero\"\n   549→\t\tag.logger.Debug(message, \"alert\", alert.Name(), \"fingerprint\", alert.Fingerprint(), \"startsAt\", alert.StartsAt)\n   550→\t\tspan.AddEvent(message,\n   551→\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   552→\t\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.alert.StartsAt\", alert.StartsAt.Format(time.RFC3339)),\n   553→\t\t\t),\n   554→\t\t)\n   555→\t\tag.resetTimer(0)\n   556→\t}\n   557→\t// Check dispatcher and alert state to determine if we should run the AG now.\n   558→\tswitch d.state.Load() {\n   559→\tcase DispatcherStateWaitingToStart:\n   560→\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Not starting Aggregation Group, dispatcher is not running\")\n   561→\t\td.logger.Debug(\"Dispatcher still waiting to start\")\n   562→\tcase DispatcherStateRunning:\n   563→\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Starting Aggregation Group\")\n   564→\t\td.runAG(ag)\n   565→\tdefault:\n   566→\t\td.logger.Warn(\"unknown state detected\", \"state\", \"unknown\")\n   567→\t}\n   568→}\n   569→\n   570→func (d *Dispatcher) runAG(ag *aggrGroup) {\n   571→\tif !ag.running.CompareAndSwap(false, true) {\n   572→\t\treturn // already running\n   573→\t}\n   574→\tgo ag.run(func(ctx context.Context, alerts ...*types.Alert) bool {\n   575→\t\t_, _, err := d.stage.Exec(ctx, d.logger, alerts...)\n   576→\t\tif err != nil {\n   577→\t\t\tlogger := d.logger.With(\"aggrGroup\", ag.GroupKey(), \"num_alerts\", len(alerts), \"err\", err)\n   578→\t\t\tif errors.Is(ctx.Err(), context.Canceled) {\n   579→\t\t\t\t// It is expected for the context to be canceled on\n   580→\t\t\t\t// configuration reload or shutdown. In this case, the\n   581→\t\t\t\t// message should only be logged at the debug level.\n   582→\t\t\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Notify for alerts failed\")\n   583→\t\t\t} else {\n   584→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"Notify for alerts failed\")\n   585→\t\t\t}\n   586→\t\t}\n   587→\t\treturn err == nil\n   588→\t})\n   589→}\n   590→\n   591→func getGroupLabels(alert *types.Alert, route *Route) model.LabelSet {\n   592→\tgroupLabels := model.LabelSet{}\n   593→\tfor ln, lv := range alert.Labels {\n   594→\t\tif _, ok := route.RouteOpts.GroupBy[ln]; ok || route.RouteOpts.GroupByAll {\n   595→\t\t\tgroupLabels[ln] = lv\n   596→\t\t}\n   597→\t}\n   598→\n   599→\treturn groupLabels\n   600→}\n   601→\n   602→// aggrGroup aggregates alert fingerprints into groups to which a\n   603→// common set of routing options applies.\n   604→// It emits notifications in the specified intervals.\n   605→type aggrGroup struct {\n   606→\tlabels   model.LabelSet\n   607→\topts     *RouteOpts\n   608→\tlogger   *slog.Logger\n   609→\trouteID  string\n   610→\trouteKey string\n   611→\n   612→\talerts  *store.Alerts\n   613→\tmarker  types.AlertMarker\n   614→\tctx     context.Context\n   615→\tcancel  func()\n   616→\tdone    chan struct{}\n   617→\tnext    *time.Timer\n   618→\ttimeout func(time.Duration) time.Duration\n   619→\trunning atomic.Bool\n   620→}\n   621→\n   622→// newAggrGroup returns a new aggregation group.\n   623→func newAggrGroup(\n   624→\tctx context.Context,\n   625→\tlabels model.LabelSet,\n   626→\tr *Route,\n   627→\tto again against all routes. The alert has already matched against this\n\t// route on ingestion.\n\treceivers := map[model.Fingerprint][]string{}\n\n\tnow := time.Now()\n\tfor i := range d.routeGroupsSlice {\n\t\tif !routeFilter(d.routeGroupsSlice[i].route) {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\treceiver := d.routeGroupsSlice[i].route.RouteOpts.Receiver\n\n\t\t// Make a snapshot of the aggregation groups in each route to avoid holding\n\t\t// sync.Map locks while we process alerts or acquiring leaf locks in the alert\n\t\t// store.\n\n\t\t// Estimate capacity based on total groups and number of routes.\n\t\t// We overallocate a bit to avoid copying in most cases.\n\t\tsnapshot := make([]*aggrGroup, 0, d.routeGroupsSlice[i].groupsLen.Load()+32)\n\t\td.routeGroupsSlice[i].groups.Range(func(_, el any) bool {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = append(snapshot, el.(*aggrGroup))\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Process the snapshot without holding sync.Map locks\n\t\tfor _, ag := range snapshot {\n\t\t\talertGroup := &AlertGroup{\n\t\t\t\tLabels:   ag.labels,\n\t\t\t\tReceiver: receiver,\n\t\t\t\tGroupKey: ag.GroupKey(),\n\t\t\t\tRouteID:  ag.routeID,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\talerts := ag.alerts.List()\n\t\t\tfilteredAlerts := make([]*types.Alert, 0, len(alerts))\n\t\t\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n\t\t\t\tif !alertFilter(a, now) {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tfp := a.Fingerprint()\n\t\t\t\tif r, ok := receivers[fp]; ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Receivers slice already exists. alert.StartsAt.Format(time.RFC3339)),\n\t\t\t),\n\t\t)\n\t\tag.resetTimer(0)\n\t}\n\t// Check dispatcher and alert state to determine if we should run the AG now.\n\tswitch d.state.Load() {\n\tcase DispatcherStateWaitingToStart:\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Not starting Aggregation Group, dispatcher is not running\")\n\t\td.logger.Debug(\"Dispatcher still waiting to start\")\n\tcase It implements the Muter\n   182→// interface.\n   183→func (ih *Inhibitor) Mutes(ctx context.Context, lset model.LabelSet) bool {\n   184→\tfp := lset.Fingerprint()\n   185→\n   186→\t_, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"inhibit.Inhibitor.Mutes\",\n   187→\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(attribute.String(\"alerting.alert.fingerprint\", fp.String())),\n   188→\t\ttrace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindInternal),\n   189→\t)\n   190→\tdefer span.End()\n   191→\n   192→\tnow := time.Now()\n   193→\tfor _, r := range ih.rules {\n   194→\t\tif !r.TargetMatchers.Matches(lset) {\n   195→\t\t\t// If target side of rule doesn't match, we don't need to look any further.\n   196→\t\t\tcontinue\n   197→\t\t}\n   198→\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"alert matched rule target\",\n   199→\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   200→\t\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.inhibit_rule.name\", r.Name),\n   201→\t\t\t),\n   202→\t\t)\n   203→\t\t// If we are here, the target side matches. If the source side matches, too, we\n   204→\t\t// need to exclude inhibiting alerts for which the same is true.\n   205→\t\tif inhibitedByFP, eq := r.hasEqual(lset, r.SourceMatchers.Matches(lset), now); eq {\n   206→\t\t\tih.marker.SetInhibited(fp, inhibitedByFP.String())\n   207→\t\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"alert inhibited\",\n   208→\t\t\t\ttrace.WithAttributes(\n   209→\t\t\t\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.inhibit_rule.source.fingerprint\", inhibitedByFP.String()),\n   210→\t\t\t\t),\n   211→\t\t\t)\n   212→\t\t\treturn true\n   213→\t\t}\n   214→\t}\n   215→\tih.marker.SetInhibited(fp)\n   216→\tspan.AddEvent(\"alert not inhibited\")\n   217→\n   218→\treturn false\n   219→}\n   220→\n   221→// An InhibitRule specifies that a class of (source) alerts should inhibit\n   222→// notifications for another class of (target) alerts if all specified matching\n   223→// labels are equal between the two alerts. This may be used to inhibit alerts\n   224→// from sending notifications if their meaning is logically a subset of a\n   225→// higher-level alert.\n   226→type InhibitRule struct {\n   227→\t// Name is an optional name for the inhibition rule.\n   228→\tName string\n   229→\t// The set of Filters which define the group of source alerts (which inhibit\n   230→\t// the target alerts).\n   231→\tSourceMatchers labels.Matchers\n   232→\t// The set of Filters which define the group of target alerts (which are\n   233→\t// inhibited by the source alerts).\n   234→\tTargetMatchers labels.Matchers\n   235→\t// A set of label names whose label values need to be identical in source and\n   236→\t// target alerts in order for the inhibition to take effect.\n   237→\tEqual map[model.LabelName]struct{}\n   238→\n   239→\t// Cache of alerts matching source labels.\n   240→\tscache *store.Alerts\n   241→\n   242→\t// Index of fingerprints of source alert equal labels to fingerprint of source alert.\n   243→\t// The index helps speed up source alert lookups from scache significantely in scenarios with 100s of source alerts cached.\n   244→\t// The index items might overwrite eachother if multiple source alerts have exact equal labels.\n   245→\t// Overwrites only happen if the new source alert has bigger EndsAt value.\n   246→\tsindex *index\n   247→}\n   248→\n   249→// NewInhibitRule returns a new InhibitRule based on a configuration definition.\n   250→func NewInhibitRule(cr config.InhibitRule) *InhibitRule {\n   251→\tvar (\n   252→\t\tsourcem labels.Matchers\n   253→\t\ttargetm labels.Matchers\n   254→\t)\n   255→\n   256→\t// cr.SourceMatch will be deprecated. This for loop appends regex matchers.\n   257→\tfor ln, lv := range cr.SourceMatch {\n   258→\t\tmatcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(labels.MatchEqual, ln, lv)\n   259→\t\tif err != nil {\n   260→\t\t\t// This error must not happen because the config already validates the yaml.\n   261→\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   262→\t\t}\n   263→\t\tsourcem = append(sourcem, matcher)\n   264→\t}\n   265→\t// cr.SourceMatchRE will be deprecated. This for loop appends regex matchers.\n   266→\tfor ln, lv := range cr.SourceMatchRE {\n   267→\t\tmatcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(labels.MatchRegexp, ln, lv.String())\n   268→\t\tif err != nil {\n   269→\t\t\t// This error must not happen because the config already validates the yaml.\n   270→\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   271→\t\t}\n   272→\t\tsourcem = append(sourcem, matcher)\n   273→\t}\n   274→\t// We append the new-style matchers. This can be simplified once the deprecated matcher syntax is removed.\n   275→\tsourcem = append(sourcem, cr.SourceMatchers...)\n   276→\n   277→\t// cr.TargetMatch will be deprecated. This for loop appends regex matchers.\n   278→\tfor ln, lv := range cr.TargetMatch {\n   279→\t\tmatcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(labels.MatchEqual, ln, lv)\n   280→\t\tif err != nil {\n   281→\t\t\t// This error must not happen because the config already validates the yaml.\n   282→\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   283→\t\t}\n   284→\t\ttargetm = append(targetm, matcher)\n   285→\t}\n   286→\t// cr.TargetMatchRE will be deprecated. This for loop appends regex matchers.\n   287→\tfor ln, lv := range cr.TargetMatchRE {\n   288→\t\tmatcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(labels.MatchRegexp, ln, lv.String())\n   289→\t\tif err != nil {\n   290→\t\t\t// This error must not happen because the config already validates the yaml.\n   291→\t\t\tpanic(err)\n   292→\t\t}\n   293→\t\ttargetm = append(targetm, matcher)\n   294→\t}\n   295→\t// We append the new-style matchers. This can be simplified once the deprecated matcher syntax is removed.\n   296→\ttargetm = append(targetm, cr.TargetMatchers...)\n   297→\n   298→\tequal := map[model.LabelName]struct{}{}\n   299→\tfor _, ln := range cr.Equal {\n   300→\t\tequal[model.LabelName(ln)] = struct{}{}\n   301→\t}\n   302→\n   303→\trule := &InhibitRule{\n   304→\t\tName:           cr.Name,\n   305→\t\tSourceMatchers: sourcem,\n   306→\t\tTargetMatchers: targetm,\n   307→\t\tEqual:          equal,\n   308→\t\tscache:         store.NewAlerts(),\n   309→\t\tsindex:         newIndex(),\n   310→\t}\n   311→\n   312→\trule.scache.SetGCCallback(rule.gcCallback)\n   313→\n   314→\treturn rule\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→// fingerprintEquals returns the fingerprint of the equal labels of the given label set.\n   318→func (r *InhibitRule) fingerprintEquals(lset model.LabelSet) model.Fingerprint {\n   319→\tequalSet := model.LabelSet{}\n   320→\tfor n := range r.Equal {\n   321→\t\tequalSet[n] = lset[n]\n   322→\t}\n   323→\treturn equalSet.Fingerprint()\n   324→}\n   325→\n   326→// updateIndex updates the source alert index if necessary.\n   327→func (r *InhibitRule) updateIndex(alert *types.Alert) {\n   328→\tfp := alert.Fingerprint()\n   329→\t// Calculate source labelset subset which is in equals.\n   330→\teq := r.fingerprintEquals(alert.Labels)\n   331→\n   332→\t// Check if the equal labelset is already in the index.\n   333→\tindexed, ok := r.sindex.Get(eq)\n   334→\tif !ok {\n   335→\t\t// If not, add it.\n   336→\t\tr.sindex.Set(eq, fp)\n   337→\t\treturn\n   338→\t}\n   339→\t// If the indexed fingerprint is the same as the new fingerprint, do nothing.\n   340→\tif indexed == fp {\n   341→\t\treturn\n   342→\t}\n   343→\n   344→\t// New alert and existing index are not the same, compare them.\n   345→\texisting, err := r.scache.Get(indexed)\n   346→\tif err != nil {\n   347→\t\t// failed to get the existing alert, overwrite the index.\n   348→\t\tr.sindex.Set(eq, fp)\n   349→\t\treturn\n   350→\t}\n   351→\n   352→\t// If the new alert resolves after the existing alert, replace the index.\n   353→\tif existing.ResolvedAt(alert.EndsAt) {\n   354→\t\tr.sindex.Set(eq, fp)\n   355→\t\treturn\n   356→\t}\n   357→\t// If the existing alert resolves after the new alert, do nothing.\n   358→}\n   359→\n   360→// findEqualSourceAlert returns the source alert that matches the equal labels of the given label set.\n   361→func (r *InhibitRule) findEqualSourceAlert(lset model.LabelSet, now time.Time) (*types.Alert, bool) {\n   362→\tequalsFP := r.fingerprintEquals(lset)\n   363→\tsourceFP, ok := r.sindex.Get(equalsFP)\n   364→\tif ok {\n   365→\t\talert, err := r.scache.Get(sourceFP)\n   366→\t\tif err != nil {\n   367→\t\t\treturn nil, false\n   368→\t\t}\n   369→\n   370→\t\tif alert.ResolvedAt(now) {\n   371→\t\t\treturn nil, false\n   372→\t\t}\n   373→\n   374→\t\treturn alert, true\n   375→\t}\n   376→\n   377→\treturn nil, false\n   378→}\n   379→\n   380→func (r *InhibitRule) gcCallback(alerts []*types.Alert) {\n   381→\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n   382→\t\tfp := r.fingerprintEquals(a.Labels)\n   383→\t\tr.sindex.Delete(fp)\n   384→\t}\n   385→}\n   386→\n   387→// hasEqual checks whether the source cache contains alerts matching the equal\n   388→// labels for the given label set. If so, the fingerprint of one of those alerts\n   389→// is returned. If excludeTwoSidedMatch is true, alerts that match both the\n   390→// source and the target side of the rule are disregarded.\n   391→func (r *InhibitRule) hasEqual(lset model.LabelSet, excludeTwoSidedMatch bool, now time.Time) (model.Fingerprint, bool) {\n   392→\tequal, found := r.findEqualSourceAlert(lset, now)\n   393→\tif found {\n   394→\t\tif excludeTwoSidedMatch && r.TargetMatchers.Matches(equal.Labels) {\n   395→\t\t\treturn model.Fingerprint(0), false\n   396→\t\t}\n   397→\t\treturn equal.Fingerprint(), found\n   398→\t}\n   399→\n   400→\treturn model.Fingerprint(0), false\n   401→}\n   402→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. need to check if those match lset or there were\n\t// silences last time we queried so we need to see if those are still active/have become\n\t// active. It's possible for there to be both old and new silences.\n\n\tif cachedEntry.count() > 0 {\n\t\t// there were old silences for this lset, we need to find them to check if they\n\t\t// are still active/pending, or have ended.\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\toldSils, _, err = s.silences.Query(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tQIDs(cachedEntry.silenceIDs...),\n\t\t\tQState(SilenceStateActive, SilenceStatePending),\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())\n\t\t\tspan.RecordError(err)\n\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\n\t\t\t\t\"Querying old silences failed, alerts might not get silenced correctly\",\n\t\t\t\t\"err\", err,\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif !cacheIsUpToDate {\n\t\t// New silences have been added since the last time the marker was updated. Do a full\n\t\t// query for any silences newer than the markerVersion that match the lset.\n\t\t// On this branch we WILL update newVersion since we can be sure we've seen any silences\n\t\t// newer than markerVersion.\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tnewSils, newVersion, err = s.silences.Query(\n\t\t\tctx,\n\t\t\tQSince(cachedEntry.version),\n\t\t\tQState(SilenceStateActive, SilenceStatePending),\n\t\t\tQMatches(lset),\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tspan.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())\n\t\t\tspan.RecordError(err)\n\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\n\t\t\t\t\"Querying silences failed, alerts might not get silenced correctly\",\n\t\t\t\t\"err\", err,\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// Note: if cacheIsUpToDate, newVersion is left at cachedEntry.version because the Query call\n\t// might already return a newer version, which is not the version our old list of\n\t// applicable silences is based on.\n\n\ttotalSilences := len(oldSils) + len(newSils)\n\tif totalSilences == 0 {\n\t\t// Easy case, neither active nor pending silences anymore.\n\t\ts.cache.set(fp, newCacheEntry(newVersion))\n\t\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, nil)\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"No silences to match\", trace.WithAttributes(\n\t\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.silences.count\", totalSilences),\n\t\t))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// It is still possible that nothing has changed, but finding out is not\n\t// much less effort than just recreating the IDs from the query\n\t// result. So let's do it in any case. Note that we cannot reuse the\n\t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\n\tactiveIDs := make([]string, 0, totalSilences)\n\tallIDs := make([]string, 0, totalSilences)\n\tseen := make(map[string]struct{}, totalSilences)\n\tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\n\n\t// Categorize old and new silences by their current state.\n\t// oldSils and newSils may overlap if a cached silence was updated\n\t// (receiving a new version), so we deduplicate by ID.\n\tfor _, sils := range [...][]*pb.Silence{oldSils, newSils} {\n\t\tfor _, sil := range sils {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := seen[sil.Id]; ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tseen[sil.Id] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\tswitch getState(sil, now) {\n\t\t\tcase SilenceStatePending:\n\t\t\t\tallIDs = append(allIDs, sil.Id)\n\t\t\tcase SilenceStateActive:\n\t\t\t\tactiveIDs = append(activeIDs, sil.Id)\n\t\t\t\tallIDs = append(allIDs, sil.Id)\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t// Do nothing, silence has expired in the meantime.\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\ts.logger.Debug(\n\t\t\"determined current silences state\",\n\t\t\"now\", now,\n\t\t\"total\", len(allIDs),\n\t\t\"active\", len(activeIDs),\n\t\t\"pending\", len(allIDs)-len(activeIDs),\n\t)\n\t// TODO: remove this sort once the marker is removed.\n\tsort.Strings(activeIDs)\n\n\ts.cache.set(fp, newCacheEntry(newVersion, allIDs...))\n\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, activeIDs)\n\n\tt := trace.WithAttributes(\n\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.silences.active.count\", len(activeIDs)),\n\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.silences.pending.count\", len(allIDs)-len(activeIDs)),\n\t\tattribute.Int(\"alerting.silences.total.count\", len(allIDs)),\n\t)\n\n\tmutes := len(activeIDs) > 0\n\tif mutes {\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Silencer mutes alert\", t)\n\t} else {\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Silencer does not mute alert\", t)\n\t}\n\treturn mutes\n}\n\n// The following methods implement mem.AlertStoreCallback.\nfunc (s *Silencer) PreStore(_ *types.Alert, _ bool) error { return nil }\nfunc (s *Silencer) PostStore(_ *types.Alert, _ bool)      {}\nfunc (s *Silencer) PostDelete(alert *types.Alert)         {}\nfunc (s *Silencer) PostGC(ff model.Fingerprints) {\n\tfor _, fp := range ff {\n\t\ts.cache.delete(fp)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Silences holds a silence state that can be modified, queried, and snapshot.\ntype Silences struct {\n\tclock quartz.Clock\n\n\tlogger    *slog.Logger\n\tmetrics   *metrics\n\tretention time.Duration\n\tlimits    Limits\n\n\tmtx       sync.RWMutex\n\tst        state\n\tversion   int // Increments whenever silences are added.\n\tbroadcast func([]byte)\n\tmi        matcherIndex\n\tvi        versionIndex\n}\n\n// Limits contains the limits for silences.\ntype Limits struct {\n\t// MaxSilences limits the maximum number of silences, including expired\n\t// silences.\n\tMaxSilences func() int\n\t// MaxSilenceSizeBytes is the maximum size of an individual silence as\n\t// stored on disk.\n\tMaxSilenceSizeBytes func() int\n}\n\n// MaintenanceFunc represents the function to run as part of the periodic maintenance for silences.\n// It returns the size of the snapshot taken or an error if it failed.\ntype MaintenanceFunc func() (int64, error)\n\ntype metrics struct {\n\tgcDuration                            prometheus.Summary\n\tgcErrorsTotal                         prometheus.Counter\n\tsnapshotDuration                      prometheus.Summary\n\tsnapshotSize                          prometheus.Gauge\n\tqueriesTotal                          prometheus.Counter\n\tqueryErrorsTotal                      prometheus.Counter\n\tqueryDuration                         prometheus.Histogram\n\tqueryScannedTotal                     prometheus.Counter\n\tquerySkippedTotal                     prometheus.Counter\n\tsilencesActive                        prometheus.GaugeFunc\n\tsilencesPending                       prometheus.GaugeFunc\n\tsilencesExpired                       prometheus.GaugeFunc\n\tstateSize                             prometheus.Gauge\n\tmatcherIndexSize                      prometheus.Gauge\n\tversionIndexSize                      prometheus.Gauge\n\tpropagatedMessagesTotal               prometheus.Counter\n\tmaintenanceTotal                      prometheus.Counter\n\tmaintenanceErrorsTotal                prometheus.Counter\n\tmatcherCompileIndexSilenceErrorsTotal prometheus.Counter\n\tmatcherCompileLoadSnapshotErrorsTotal prometheus.Counter\n}\n\nfunc newSilenceMetricByState(r prometheus.Registerer, s *Silences, st SilenceState) prometheus.GaugeFunc {\n\treturn promauto.With(r).NewGaugeFunc(\n\t\tprometheus.GaugeOpts{\n\t\t\tName:        \"alertmanager_silences\",\n\t\t\tHelp:        \"How many silences by state.\",\n\t\t\tConstLabels: prometheus.Labels{\"state\": string(st)},\n\t\t},\n\t\tfunc() float64 {\n\t\t\tcount, err := s.CountState(context.Background(), st)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Counting silences failed\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn float64(count)\n\t\t},\n\t)\n}\n\nfunc newMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer, s *Silences) *metrics {\n\tm := &metrics{}\n\n\tm.gcDuration = promauto.With(r).NewSummary(prometheus.SummaryOpts{\n\t\tName:       \"alertmanager_silences_gc_duration_seconds\",\n\t\tHelp:       \"Duration of the last silence garbage collection cycle.\",\n\t\tObjectives: map[float64]float64{},\n\t})\n\tm.gcErrorsTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_gc_errors_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"How many silence GC errors were encountered.\",\n\t})\n\tm.snapshotDuration = promauto.With(r).NewSummary(prometheus.SummaryOpts{\n\t\tName:       \"alertmanager_silences_snapshot_duration_seconds\",\n\t\tHelp:       \"Duration of the last silence snapshot.\",\n\t\tObjectives: map[float64]float64{},\n\t})\n\tm.snapshotSize = promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_snapshot_size_bytes\",\n\t\tHelp: \"Size of the last silence snapshot in bytes.\",\n\t})\n\tm.maintenanceTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_maintenance_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"How many maintenances were executed for silences.\",\n\t})\n\tm.maintenanceErrorsTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_maintenance_errors_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"How many maintenances were executed for silences that failed.\",\n\t})\n\tmatcherCompileErrorsTotal := promauto.With(r).NewCounterVec(\n\t\tprometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_matcher_compile_errors_total\",\n\t\t\tHelp: \"How many silence matcher compilations failed.\",\n\t\t},\n\t\t[]string{\"stage\"},\n\t)\n\tm.matcherCompileIndexSilenceErrorsTotal = matcherCompileErrorsTotal.WithLabelValues(\"index\")\n\tm.matcherCompileLoadSnapshotErrorsTotal = many silence received queries did not succeed.\",\n\t})\n\tm.queryDuration = promauto.With(r).NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n\t\tName:                            \"alertmanager_silences_query_duration_seconds\",\n\t\tHelp:                            \"Duration of silence query evaluation.\",\n\t\tBuckets:                         prometheus.DefBuckets,\n\t\tNativeHistogramBucketFactor:     1.1,\n\t\tNativeHistogramMaxBucketNumber:  100,\n\t\tNativeHistogramMinResetDuration: 1 * time.Hour,\n\t})\n\tm.queryScannedTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_query_silences_scanned_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"How many silences were scanned during query evaluation.\",\n\t})\n\tm.querySkippedTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_query_silences_skipped_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"How many silences were skipped during query evaluation using the version index.\",\n\t})\n\tm.propagatedMessagesTotal = promauto.With(r).NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_gossip_messages_propagated_total\",\n\t\tHelp: \"Number of received gossip messages that have been further gossiped.\",\n\t})\n\tif s != nil {\n\t\tm.silencesActive = newSilenceMetricByState(r, s, SilenceStateActive)\n\t\tm.silencesPending = newSilenceMetricByState(r, s, SilenceStatePending)\n\t\tm.silencesExpired = newSilenceMetricByState(r, s, SilenceStateExpired)\n\t\tm.stateSize = promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n\t\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_state_size\",\n\t\t\tHelp: \"The number of silences in the state map.\",\n\t\t})\n\t\tm.matcherIndexSize = promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n\t\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_matcher_index_size\",\n\t\t\tHelp: \"The number of entries in the matcher cache index.\",\n\t\t})\n\t\tm.versionIndexSize = promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n\t\t\tName: \"alertmanager_silences_version_index_size\",\n\t\t\tHelp: \"The number of entries in the version index.\",\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn m\n}\n\n// Options exposes configuration options for creating a new Silences object.\n// Its zero value is a safe default.\ntype Options struct {\n\t// A snapshot file or reader from which the initial state is loaded.\n\t// None or only one of them must be set.\n\tSnapshotFile   string\n\tSnapshotReader io.Reader\n\n\t// Retention time for newly created Silences. Silences may be\n\t// garbage collected after the given duration after they ended.\n\tRetention time.Duration\n\tLimits    Limits\n\n\t// A logger used by background processing.\n\tLogger  *slog.Logger\n\tMetrics prometheus.Registerer\n}\n\nfunc (o *Options) validate() error {\n\tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" && o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"only one of SnapshotFile and SnapshotReader must be set\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// New returns a new Silences object with the given configuration.\nfunc New(o Options) (*Silences, error) {\n\tif err := o.validate(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ts := &Silences{\n\t\tclock:     quartz.NewReal(),\n\t\tmi:        make(matcherIndex, 512),\n\t\tvi:        make(versionIndex, 0, 512),\n\t\tlogger:    promslog.NewNopLogger(),\n\t\tretention: o.Retention,\n\t\tlimits:    o.Limits,\n\t\tbroadcast: func([]byte) {},\n\t\tst:        state{},\n\t}\n\tif o.Metrics == nil {\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"Options.Metrics is nil\")\n\t}\n\ts.metrics = newMetrics(o.Metrics, s)\n\n\tif o.Logger != nil {\n\t\ts.logger = o.Logger\n\t}\n\n\tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" {\n\t\tif r, err := os.Open(o.SnapshotFile); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"silences snapshot file doesn't exist\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\to.SnapshotReader = r\n\t\t\tdefer r.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n\t\tif err := s.loadSnapshot(o.SnapshotReader); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn s, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn s, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) nowUTC() time.Time {\n\treturn s.clock.Now().UTC()\n}\n\n// updateSizeMetrics updates the size metrics for state, matcher index, and version index.\n// Must be called while holding s.mtx.\nfunc (s *Silences) updateSizeMetrics() {\n\tif s.metrics != nil && s.metrics.stateSize != nil {\n\t\ts.metrics.stateSize.Set(float64(len(s.st)))\n\t\ts.metrics.matcherIndexSize.Set(float64(len(s.mi)))\n\t\ts.metrics.versionIndexSize.Set(float64(len(s.vi)))\n\t}\n}\n\n// Maintenance garbage collects the silence state at the given interval. If the snapshot\n// file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\n// Terminates on receiving from stopc.\n// If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\nfunc (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\n\tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\n\tdefer t.Stop()\n\n\tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\n\tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\n\t\tvar size int64\n\n\t\tif _, err := s.GC(); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn size, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif snapf == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn size, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tf, err := openReplace(snapf)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn size, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif size, err = s.Snapshot(f); err != nil {\n\t\t\tf.Close()\n\t\t\treturn size, err\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn size, f.Close()\n\t}\n\n\tif override != nil {\n\t\tdoMaintenance = override\n\t}\n\n\trunMaintenance := func(do MaintenanceFunc) error {\n\t\ts.metrics.maintenanceTotal.Inc()\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Running maintenance\")\n\t\tstart := s.nowUTC()\n\t\tsize, err := do()\n\t\ts.metrics.snapshotSize.Set(float64(size))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.metrics.maintenanceErrorsTotal.Inc()\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Maintenance done\", \"duration\", s.clock.Since(start), \"size\", size)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\nLoop:\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-stopc:\n\t\t\tbreak Loop\n\t\tcase <-t.C:\n\t\t\tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Running maintenance failed\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// No need for final maintenance if we don't want to snapshot.\n\tif snapf == \"\" {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Creating shutdown snapshot failed\", \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\n// GC runs a garbage collection that removes silences that have ended longer\n// than the configured retention time ago.\nfunc (s *Silences) GC() (int, error) {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\tdefer func() { s.metrics.gcDuration.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds()) }()\n\n\tnow := s.nowUTC()\n\tvar n int\n\tvar errs error\n\n\ts.mtx.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\t// During GC we will delete expired silences from the state map and the indices.\n\t// If between the last GC's deletion, and including any silences that were added\n\t// until now, we have more than 50% spare capacity, we want to reallocate to a smaller\n\t// slice, while still leaving some growth buffer.\n\tneedsRealloc := cap(s.vi) > 1024 && len(s.vi) < cap(s.vi)/2\n\n\tvar targetVi versionIndex\n\tif needsRealloc {\n\t\t// Allocate new slice with growth buffer.\n\t\tnewCap := max(len(s.vi)*5/4, 1024)\n\t\ttargetVi = make(versionIndex, 0, newCap)\n\t} else {\n\t\ttargetVi = s.vi[:0]\n\t}\n\n\t// Iterate state map directly (fast - no extra lookups).\n\tfor _, sv := range s.vi {\n\t\tsil, ok := s.st[sv.id]\n\t\texpire := false\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t// Silence in version index but not in state - remove from version index and count error\n\t\t\ts.metrics.gcErrorsTotal.Inc()\n\t\t\terrs = errors.Join(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"silence %s in version index missing from state\", sv.id))\n\t\t\t// not adding to targetVi effectively removes it\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif sil.ExpiresAt == nil || sil.ExpiresAt.AsTime().IsZero() {\n\t\t\t// Invalid expiration timestamp - remove silence and count error\n\t\t\ts.metrics.gcErrorsTotal.Inc()\n\t\t\terrs = errors.Join(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"silence %s has zero expiration timestamp\", sil.Silence.Id))\n\t\t\texpire = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif expire || !sil.ExpiresAt.AsTime().After(now) {\n\t\t\tdelete(s.st, sil.Silence.Id)\n\t\t\tdelete(s.mi, sil.Silence.Id)\n\t\t\tn++\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ttargetVi = append(targetVi, sv)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif !needsRealloc {\n\t\t// If we didn't reallocate, clear tail to prevent string pointer leaks\n\t\tclear(s.vi[len(targetVi):])\n\t}\n\ts.vi = targetVi\n\ts.updateSizeMetrics()\n\n\treturn n, errs\n}\n\nfunc validateMatcher(m *pb.Matcher) error {\n\tif !compat.IsValidLabelName(model.LabelName(m.Name)) {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label name %q\", m.Name)\n\t}\n\tswitch m.Type {\n\tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL, pb.Matcher_NOT_EQUAL:\n\t\tif !model.LabelValue(m.Pattern).IsValid() {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label value %q\", m.Pattern)\n\t\t}\n\tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP, pb.Matcher_NOT_REGEXP:\n\t\tif _, err := regexp.Compile(m.Pattern); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid regular expression %q: %w\", m.Pattern, err)\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown matcher type %q\", m.Type)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc matchesEmpty(m *pb.Matcher) bool {\n\tswitch m.Type {\n\tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL:\n\t\treturn m.Pattern == \"\"\n\tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP:\n\t\tmatched, _ := regexp.MatchString(m.Pattern, \"\")\n\t\treturn matched\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc validateSilence(s *pb.Silence) error {\n\t// Convert old-style Matchers to MatcherSets for backward compatibility\n\tpostprocessUnmarshalledSilence(s)\n\n\tif len(s.MatcherSets) == 0 {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"at least one matcher set required\")\n\t}\n\n\tfor setIdx, ms := range s.MatcherSets {\n\t\tif len(ms.Matchers) == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"matcher set %d is empty\", setIdx)\n\t\t}\n\t\tallMatchEmpty := true\n\n\t\tfor i, m := range ms.Matchers {\n\t\t\tif err := validateMatcher(m); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label matcher %d in set %d: %w\", i, setIdx, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tallMatchEmpty = allMatchEmpty && matchesEmpty(m)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif allMatchEmpty {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"matcher set %d: at least one matcher must not match the empty string\", setIdx)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif s.StartsAt == nil || s.StartsAt.AsTime().IsZero() {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid zero start timestamp\")\n\t}\n\tif s.EndsAt == nil || s.EndsAt.AsTime().IsZero() {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid zero end timestamp\")\n\t}\n\tif s.EndsAt.AsTime().Before(s.StartsAt.AsTime()) {\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"end time must not be before start time\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// cloneSilence returns a copy of a silence.\nfunc cloneSilence(sil *pb.Silence) *pb.Silence {\n\treturn proto.Clone(sil).(*pb.Silence)\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) checkSizeLimits(msil *pb.MeshSilence) error {\n\tif s.limits.MaxSilenceSizeBytes != nil {\n\t\tn := proto.Size(msil)\n\t\tif m := s.limits.MaxSilenceSizeBytes(); m > 0 && n > m {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"silence exceeded maximum size: %d bytes (limit: %d bytes)\", n, m)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) indexSilence(sil *pb.Silence) {\n\ts.version++\n\ts.vi.add(s.version, sil.Id)\n\t_, err := s.mi.add(sil)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.metrics.matcherCompileIndexSilenceErrorsTotal.Inc()\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to compile silence matchers\", \"silence_id\", sil.Id, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) getSilence(id string) (*pb.Silence, bool) {\n\tmsil, ok := s.st[id]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn nil, false\n\t}\n\treturn msil.Silence, true\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) toMeshSilence(sil *pb.Silence) *pb.MeshSilence {\n\treturn &pb.MeshSilence{\n\t\tSilence:   sil,\n\t\tExpiresAt: timestamppb.New(sil.EndsAt.AsTime().Add(s.retention)),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Silences) setSilence(msil *pb.MeshSilence, now time.Time) error {\n\tb, err := marshalMeshSilence(msil)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\t_, added := s.st.merge(msil, now)\n\tif added {\n\t\ts.indexSilence(msil.Silence)\n\t\ts.updateSizeMetrics()\n\t}\n\ts.broadcast(b)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Set the specified silence. If a silence with the ID already exists and the modification\n// modifies history, the old silence gets expired and a new one is created.\nfunc (s *Silences) Set(ctx context.Context, sil *pb.Silence) error {\n\t_, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"silences.Set\")\n\tdefer span.End()\n\n\tnow := s.nowUTC()\n\tif sil.StartsAt == nil || sil.StartsAt.AsTime().IsZero() {\n\t\tsil.StartsAt = timestamppb.New(now)\n\t}\n\n\tif err := validateSilence(sil); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid silence: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\ts.mtx.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\tprev, ok := s.getSilence(sil.Id)\n\tif sil.Id != \"\" && !ok {\n\t\treturn ErrNotFound\n\t}\n\n\tif ok && canUpdate(prev, sil, now) {\n\t\tsil.UpdatedAt = timestamppb.New(now)\n\t\tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n\t\tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n\t}\n\n\t// If we got here it's either a new silence or a m > 0 && len(s.st)+1 > m {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exceeded maximum number of silences: %d (limit: %d)\", len(s.st), m)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tuid, err := uuid.NewRandom()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"generate uuid: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tsil.Id = uid.String()\n\n\tif sil.StartsAt.AsTime().Before(now) {\n\t\tsil.StartsAt = timestamppb.New(now)\n\t}\n\tsil.UpdatedAt = timestamppb.New(now)\n\n\tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n\tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tif ok && getState(prev, s.nowUTC()) != SilenceStateExpired {\n\t\t// We cannot update the silence, expire the old one to leave a history of\n\t\t// the silence before modification.\n\t\tif err := s.expire(prev.Id); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expire previous silence: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n}\n\n// canUpdate returns true if silence a can be updated to b without\n// affecting the historic view of {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\t// Allowed timestamp modifications depend on the current time.\n\tswitch st := getState(a, now); st {\n\tcase SilenceStateActive:\n\t\tif a.StartsAt.AsTime().Unix() != b.StartsAt.AsTime().Unix() {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\tif b.EndsAt.AsTime().Before(now) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\tcase SilenceStatePending:\n\t\tif b.StartsAt.AsTime().Before(now) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\tcase SilenceStateExpired:\n\t\treturn false\n\tdefault:\n\t\tpanic(\"unknown silence state\")\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\nfunc (s *Silences) Expire(ctx context.Context, id string) error {\n\ts.mtx.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\t_, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \"silences.Expire\", trace.WithAttributes(\n\t\tattribute.String(\"alerting.silence.id\", id),\n\t))\n\tdefer span.End()\n\n\treturn s.expire(id)\n}\n\n// Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\n// It is idempotent, nil is returned if the silence already expired before it is GC'd.\n// If the silence is not found an error is returned.\nfunc (s *Silences) expire(id string) error {\n\tsil, ok := s.getSilence(id)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn ErrNotFound\n\t}\n\tsil = cloneSilence(sil)\n\tnow := s.nowUTC()\n\n\tswitch getState(sil, now) {\n\tcase SilenceStateExpired:\n\t\treturn nil\n\tcase {\n\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tq.filters = append(q.filters, f)\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// QueryOne queries with the given parameters and returns the In case of a filter error, the error is returned.\n\tappendIfFiltersMatch := func(res []*pb.Silence, sil *pb.Silence) ([]*pb.Silence, error) {\n\t\tfor _, f := range q.filters {\n\t\t\tmatches, err := f(sil, s, now)\n\t\t\t// In case of error return it immediately and don't process further filters.\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn res, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// If one filter doesn't match, return the result unchanged, immediately.\n\t\t\tif !matches {\n\t\t\t\treturn res, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\t// All filters matched, append the silence to the result.\n\t\treturn append(res, cloneSilence(sil)), nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Preallocate result slice if we have IDs (if not this will be a no-op)\n\tres = make([]*pb.Silence, 0, len(q.ids))\n\n\t// Take a read lock on Silences: we can read but not modify the Silences struct.\n\ts.mtx.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mtx.RUnlock()\n\n\t// If we have IDs, only consider the silences with the given IDs, if they exist.\n\tif q.ids != nil {\n\t\tfor _, id := range q.ids {\n\t\t\tif sil, ok := s.st[id]; ok {\n\t\t\t\tscannedCount++\n\t\t\t\t// append the silence to the results if it satisfies the query.\n\t\t\t\tres, err = appendIfFiltersMatch(res, sil.Silence)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, s.version, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tstart := 0\n\t\tif q.since != nil {\n\t\t\tvar found bool\n\t\t\tstart, found = s.vi.findVersionGreaterThan(*q.since)\n\t\t\t// no new silences, nothing to do\n\t\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\t\treturn res, s.version, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Track how many silences we skipped using the version index.\n\t\t\ts.metrics.querySkippedTotal.Add(float64(start))\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Preallocate result slice with a reasonable capacity.
